pharmaceuticals outfit a boutique company in stock market jargonthat did research on viruses that could kill security was deadly serious toni had organized a spot check of supplies and had found that two doses of an experimental drug were missing that was bad enough the drug an antiviral agent was top secret its formula priceless it might have been stolen for sale to a rival company but another
